/* check session */
declare @project_admin int
select @project_admin = count(1)
	from sessions
	inner join project_user_xref on pu_user = se_user
	and pu_admin = 1
	where se_id = '4485040b-59c5-457f-8efa-b4309e3e69dd';

select us_id, us_admin,
us_username, us_firstname, us_lastname,
isnull(us_email,'') us_email,
isnull(us_bugs_per_page,10) us_bugs_per_page,
isnull(us_forced_project,0) us_forced_project,
us_use_fckeditor,
us_enable_bug_list_popups,
og.*,
isnull(us_forced_project, 0 ) us_forced_project,
isnull(pu_permission_level, 2) pu_permission_level,
@project_admin [project_admin]
from sessions
inner join users on se_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
left outer join project_user_xref
	on pu_project = us_forced_project
	and pu_user = us_id
where se_id = '4485040b-59c5-457f-8efa-b4309e3e69dd'
and us_active = 1

/* drop downs */ select pj_id, pj_name
		from projects
		left outer join project_user_xref on pj_id = pu_project
		and pu_user = 3
		where pj_active = 1
		and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) not in (0, 1)
		order by pj_name;
select og_id, og_name from orgs where og_active = 1 order by og_name;
select ct_id, ct_name from categories order by ct_sort_seq, ct_name;
select pr_id, pr_name from priorities order by pr_sort_seq, pr_name;
select st_id, st_name from statuses order by st_sort_seq, st_name;
select udf_id, udf_name from user_defined_attribute order by udf_sort_seq, udf_name;

select top 1 pj_id from projects where pj_default = 1 order by pj_name;
select top 1 ct_id from categories where ct_default = 1 order by ct_name;
select top 1 pr_id from priorities where pr_default = 1 order by pr_name;
select top 1 st_id from statuses where st_default = 1 order by st_name;
select top 1 udf_id from user_defined_attribute where udf_default = 1 order by udf_name;

2016-04-15 16:03:51 http://www.learncodinganywhere.com/bugtracker/edit_bug.aspx sql=

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
where us_active = 1
and og_can_be_assigned_to = 1
and (0 <> 0 or 4 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 0
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

2016-04-15 16:45:14 http://www.learncodinganywhere.com/bugtracker/ajax.aspx?bugid=212 elapsed milliseconds:0001
2016-04-15 16:45:14 http://www.learncodinganywhere.com/bugtracker/ajax.aspx?bugid=212 sql=

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 212
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 and a.bp_hidden_from_external_users = 0
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id
2016-04-15 16:45:14 http://www.learncodinganywhere.com/bugtracker/ajax.aspx?bugid=212 elapsed milliseconds:0001

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username

and (0 <> 0 or 4 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 0
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

declare @pj int
select @pj = bg_project from bugs where bg_id = 210

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 210
and bs_user in
(select x.pu_user
from projects
left outer join project_user_xref x on pu_project = pj_id
where pu_project = @pj
and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) = 0)

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 210
and bs_user in
(select us_id from users
 inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
 inner join bugs on bg_id = 210
 where og_other_orgs_permission_level = 0
 and bg_org <> og_id)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 210, us_id
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = 210
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_project = @pj and pu_user = us_id
where us_auto_subscribe = 1
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and us_id not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 210)

and pj_default_user <> 0
and pj_auto_subscribe_default_user = 1
and us_active = 1
and pj_default_user not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 210)

/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (2 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_assigned_notifications and 0 = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 210
and (us_id <> 3 or isnull(us_send_notifications_to_self,0) = 1)

/* get searchable cols */					
select sc.name
from syscolumns sc
inner join systypes st on st.xusertype = sc.xusertype
inner join sysobjects so on sc.id = so.id
where so.name = 'bugs'
and st.[name] <> 'sysname'
and sc.name not in ('rowguid',
'bg_id',
'bg_short_desc',
'bg_reported_user',
'bg_reported_date',
'bg_project',
'bg_org',
'bg_category',
'bg_priority',
'bg_status',
'bg_assigned_to_user',
'bg_last_updated_user',
'bg_last_updated_date',
'bg_user_defined_attribute',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3',
'bg_tags')
and st.[name] in ('nvarchar','varchar')
and sc.length > 30

bg_short_desc [short_desc],
isnull(bg_tags,'') [bg_tags],
isnull(ru.us_username,'[deleted user]') [reporter],
isnull(ru.us_email,'') [reporter_email],
case rtrim(ru.us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(ru.us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(ru.us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(ru.us_lastname + ', ' + ru.us_firstname,'')
	end [reporter_fullname],
bg_reported_date [reported_date],
datediff(s,bg_reported_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
isnull(lu.us_username,'') [last_updated_user],
case rtrim(lu.us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(lu.us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(lu.us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(lu.us_lastname + ', ' + lu.us_firstname,'')
	end [last_updated_fullname],


bg_last_updated_date [last_updated_date],
isnull(bg_project,0) [project],
isnull(pj_name,'[no project]') [current_project],

isnull(bg_org,0) [organization],
isnull(bugorg.og_name,'') [og_name],

isnull(bg_category,0) [category],
isnull(ct_name,'') [category_name],

isnull(bg_priority,0) [priority],
isnull(pr_name,'') [priority_name],

isnull(bg_status,0) [status],
isnull(st_name,'') [status_name],

isnull(bg_user_defined_attribute,0) [udf],
isnull(udf_name,'') [udf_name],

isnull(bg_assigned_to_user,0) [assigned_to_user],
isnull(asg.us_username,'[not assigned]') [assigned_to_username],
case rtrim(asg.us_firstname)
when null then isnull(asg.us_lastname, '[not assigned]')
when '' then isnull(asg.us_lastname, '[not assigned]')
else isnull(asg.us_lastname + ', ' + asg.us_firstname,'[not assigned]')
end [assigned_to_fullname],

isnull(bs_user,0) [subscribed],

case
when
	4 <> bg_org
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
		then userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
	isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end [pu_permission_level],

isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1],
isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2],
isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3],
@related [relationship_cnt],
@svn_revisions [svn_revision_cnt],
@git_commits [git_commit_cnt],
@hg_revisions [hg_commit_cnt],
@tasks [task_cnt],
getdate() [snapshot_timestamp]

from bugs
inner join users this_user on us_id = 3
inner join orgs userorg on this_user.us_org = userorg.og_id
left outer join user_defined_attribute on bg_user_defined_attribute = udf_id
left outer join projects on bg_project = pj_id
left outer join orgs bugorg on bg_org = bugorg.og_id
left outer join categories on bg_category = ct_id
left outer join priorities on bg_priority = pr_id
left outer join statuses on bg_status = st_id

left outer join users ru on bg_reported_user = ru.us_id
left outer join users lu on bg_last_updated_user = lu.us_id
left outer join bug_subscriptions on bs_bug = bg_id and bs_user = 3
left outer join project_user_xref on pj_id = pu_project
and pu_user = 3
where bg_id = 210

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
where us_active = 1
and og_can_be_assigned_to = 1
and (0 <> 0 or 4 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 0
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
where us_active = 1
and og_can_be_assigned_to = 1
and (0 <> 0 or 4 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 0
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 211
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 and a.bp_hidden_from_external_users = 0
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (2 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_assigned_notifications and 0 = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 211
and (us_id <> 3 or isnull(us_send_notifications_to_self,0) = 1)

/* get searchable cols */

from syscolumns sc
inner join systypes st on st.xusertype = sc.xusertype

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
where us_active = 1
and og_can_be_assigned_to = 1
and (0 <> 0 or 4 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 0
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 211
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 and a.bp_hidden_from_external_users = 0
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

	end [last_updated_fullname],

isnull(st_name,'') [status_name],

when '' then isnull(asg.us_lastname, '[not assigned]')
else isnull(asg.us_lastname + ', ' + asg.us_firstname,'[not assigned]')
end [assigned_to_fullname],

isnull(bs_user,0) [subscribed],

case
when
	4 <> bg_org
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
		then userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
	isnull(pu_permission_level,2)

@related [relationship_cnt],
@svn_revisions [svn_revision_cnt],
@git_commits [git_commit_cnt],
@hg_revisions [hg_commit_cnt],
@tasks [task_cnt],
getdate() [snapshot_timestamp]

and pu_user = 3
where bg_id = 212

declare @pj int
select @pj = bg_project from bugs where bg_id = 212

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 212
and bs_user in
(select x.pu_user
from projects
left outer join project_user_xref x on pu_project = pj_id
where pu_project = @pj
and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) = 0)

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 212
and bs_user in
(select us_id from users
 inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
 inner join bugs on bg_id = 212
 where og_other_orgs_permission_level = 0
 and bg_org <> og_id)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 212, us_id
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = 212
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_project = @pj and pu_user = us_id
where us_auto_subscribe = 1
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and us_id not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 212)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 212, pj_default_user
from projects
inner join users on pj_default_user = us_id
where pj_id = @pj
and pj_default_user <> 0
and pj_auto_subscribe_default_user = 1
and us_active = 1
and pj_default_user not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 212)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 212, pu_user from project_user_xref
inner join users on pu_user = us_id
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = 212
where pu_auto_subscribe = 1
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and pu_project = @pj
and pu_user not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 212)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 212, us_id
from users
inner join bugs on bg_id = 212
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_project = @pj and pu_user = us_id
where ((us_auto_subscribe_own_bugs = 1 and bg_assigned_to_user = us_id)
or
(us_auto_subscribe_reported_bugs = 1 and bg_reported_user = us_id))
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and us_id not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 212)

/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (2 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_assigned_notifications and 0 = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 212
and (us_id <> 3 or isnull(us_send_notifications_to_self,0) = 1)

/* get searchable cols */					
select sc.name
from syscolumns sc
inner join systypes st on st.xusertype = sc.xusertype
inner join sysobjects so on sc.id = so.id
where so.name = 'bugs'
and st.[name] <> 'sysname'
and sc.name not in ('rowguid',
'bg_id',
'bg_short_desc',
'bg_reported_user',
'bg_reported_date',
'bg_project',
'bg_org',
'bg_category',
'bg_priority',
'bg_status',
'bg_assigned_to_user',
'bg_last_updated_user',
'bg_last_updated_date',
'bg_user_defined_attribute',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3',
'bg_tags')
and st.[name] in ('nvarchar','varchar')
and sc.length > 30

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 212
and a.bp_parent is null
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
where us_active = 1
and og_can_be_assigned_to = 1
and (0 <> 0 or 4 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 0
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (1 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (1 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (1 <= us_assigned_notifications and 0 = bs_user)
or (1 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 213
and (us_id <> 3 or isnull(us_send_notifications_to_self,0) = 1)

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username
from users

where us_active = 1
and og_can_be_assigned_to = 1
and (0 <> 0 or 4 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 0
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
where us_active = 1
and og_can_be_assigned_to = 1
and (0 <> 0 or 4 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 0
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 209
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 and a.bp_hidden_from_external_users = 0
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

declare @pj int
select @pj = bg_project from bugs where bg_id = 209

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 209
and bs_user in
(select x.pu_user
from projects
left outer join project_user_xref x on pu_project = pj_id
where pu_project = @pj
and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) = 0)

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 209
and bs_user in
(select us_id from users
 inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
 inner join bugs on bg_id = 209
 where og_other_orgs_permission_level = 0
 and bg_org <> og_id)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 209, us_id
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = 209
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_project = @pj and pu_user = us_id
where us_auto_subscribe = 1
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and us_id not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 209)

/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (2 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_assigned_notifications and 0 = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 209
and (us_id <> 3 or isnull(us_send_notifications_to_self,0) = 1)

/* get searchable cols */					
select sc.name
from syscolumns sc
inner join systypes st on st.xusertype = sc.xusertype
inner join sysobjects so on sc.id = so.id
where so.name = 'bugs'
and st.[name] <> 'sysname'
and sc.name not in ('rowguid',
'bg_id',
'bg_short_desc',
'bg_reported_user',
'bg_reported_date',
'bg_project',
'bg_org',
'bg_category',
'bg_priority',
'bg_status',
'bg_assigned_to_user',
'bg_last_updated_user',
'bg_last_updated_date',
'bg_user_defined_attribute',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3',
'bg_tags')
and st.[name] in ('nvarchar','varchar')
and sc.length > 30

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
where us_active = 1
and og_can_be_assigned_to = 1
and (0 <> 0 or 4 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 0
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

declare @pj int
select @pj = bg_project from bugs where bg_id = 208

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 208
and bs_user in
(select x.pu_user
from projects
left outer join project_user_xref x on pu_project = pj_id
where pu_project = @pj
and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) = 0)

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 208
and bs_user in
(select us_id from users
 inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
 inner join bugs on bg_id = 208
 where og_other_orgs_permission_level = 0
 and bg_org <> og_id)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 208, us_id
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = 208
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_project = @pj and pu_user = us_id
where us_auto_subscribe = 1
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and us_id not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 208)

and pj_default_user <> 0
and pj_auto_subscribe_default_user = 1
and us_active = 1
and pj_default_user not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 208)

/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (4 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (4 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (4 <= us_assigned_notifications and 0 = bs_user)
or (4 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 208
and (us_id <> 3 or isnull(us_send_notifications_to_self,0) = 1)

'bg_tags')

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 208
and a.bp_parent is null
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

@tasks [task_cnt],

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username

	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 0
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')

a.bp_date,

a.bp_type,

isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 208
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 and a.bp_hidden_from_external_users = 0
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 205
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 and a.bp_hidden_from_external_users = 0
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

declare @pj int
select @pj = bg_project from bugs where bg_id = 205

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 205
and bs_user in
(select x.pu_user
from projects
left outer join project_user_xref x on pu_project = pj_id
where pu_project = @pj
and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) = 0)

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 205
and bs_user in
(select us_id from users
 inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
 inner join bugs on bg_id = 205
 where og_other_orgs_permission_level = 0
 and bg_org <> og_id)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 205, us_id
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = 205
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_project = @pj and pu_user = us_id
where us_auto_subscribe = 1
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and us_id not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 205)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 205, pj_default_user
from projects
inner join users on pj_default_user = us_id
where pj_id = @pj
and pj_default_user <> 0
and pj_auto_subscribe_default_user = 1
and us_active = 1
and pj_default_user not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 205)

	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and pu_project = @pj
and pu_user not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 205)

/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (2 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_assigned_notifications and 0 = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 205
and (us_id <> 3 or isnull(us_send_notifications_to_self,0) = 1)

/* get searchable cols */					
select sc.name
from syscolumns sc
inner join systypes st on st.xusertype = sc.xusertype

and sc.name not in ('rowguid',
'bg_id',
'bg_short_desc',
'bg_reported_user',
'bg_reported_date',

'bg_org',

'bg_user_defined_attribute',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3',
'bg_tags')
and st.[name] in ('nvarchar','varchar')
and sc.length > 30

isnull(bg_assigned_to_user,0) [assigned_to_user],
isnull(asg.us_username,'[not assigned]') [assigned_to_username],
case rtrim(asg.us_firstname)
when null then isnull(asg.us_lastname, '[not assigned]')
when '' then isnull(asg.us_lastname, '[not assigned]')
else isnull(asg.us_lastname + ', ' + asg.us_firstname,'[not assigned]')
end [assigned_to_fullname],

isnull(bs_user,0) [subscribed],

case
when
	4 <> bg_org
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
		then userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
	isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end [pu_permission_level],

isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1],
isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2],
isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3],
@related [relationship_cnt],
@svn_revisions [svn_revision_cnt],
@git_commits [git_commit_cnt],
@hg_revisions [hg_commit_cnt],
@tasks [task_cnt],
getdate() [snapshot_timestamp]

from bugs
inner join users this_user on us_id = 3
inner join orgs userorg on this_user.us_org = userorg.og_id
left outer join user_defined_attribute on bg_user_defined_attribute = udf_id
left outer join projects on bg_project = pj_id
left outer join orgs bugorg on bg_org = bugorg.og_id
left outer join categories on bg_category = ct_id
left outer join priorities on bg_priority = pr_id
left outer join statuses on bg_status = st_id
left outer join users asg on bg_assigned_to_user = asg.us_id
left outer join users ru on bg_reported_user = ru.us_id
left outer join users lu on bg_last_updated_user = lu.us_id
left outer join bug_subscriptions on bs_bug = bg_id and bs_user = 3
left outer join project_user_xref on pj_id = pu_project
and pu_user = 3
where bg_id = 205

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
where us_active = 1
and og_can_be_assigned_to = 1
and (0 <> 0 or 4 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 0
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 205
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 and a.bp_hidden_from_external_users = 0
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 207
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 and a.bp_hidden_from_external_users = 0
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

where bs_bug = 214

(select x.pu_user

and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) = 0)

where bs_bug = 214
and bs_user in
(select us_id from users
 inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
 inner join bugs on bg_id = 214
 where og_other_orgs_permission_level = 0
 and bg_org <> og_id)

from users

/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (1 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (1 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (1 <= us_assigned_notifications and 0 = bs_user)
or (1 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 214
and (us_id <> 3 or isnull(us_send_notifications_to_self,0) = 1)

from syscolumns sc
inner join systypes st on st.xusertype = sc.xusertype

'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3',
'bg_tags')
and st.[name] in ('nvarchar','varchar')

	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')

	end [us_fullname],

a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 214
and a.bp_parent is null
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
where us_active = 1
and og_can_be_assigned_to = 1
and (0 <> 0 or 4 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 0
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

declare @pj int
select @pj = bg_project from bugs where bg_id = 214

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 214
and bs_user in
(select x.pu_user
from projects
left outer join project_user_xref x on pu_project = pj_id
where pu_project = @pj
and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) = 0)

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 214
and bs_user in
(select us_id from users
 inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
 inner join bugs on bg_id = 214
 where og_other_orgs_permission_level = 0
 and bg_org <> og_id)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 214, us_id
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = 214
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_project = @pj and pu_user = us_id
where us_auto_subscribe = 1
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and us_id not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 214)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 214, pj_default_user
from projects
inner join users on pj_default_user = us_id
where pj_id = @pj
and pj_default_user <> 0
and pj_auto_subscribe_default_user = 1
and us_active = 1
and pj_default_user not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 214)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 214, pu_user from project_user_xref
inner join users on pu_user = us_id
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = 214
where pu_auto_subscribe = 1
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and pu_project = @pj
and pu_user not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 214)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 214, us_id
from users
inner join bugs on bg_id = 214
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_project = @pj and pu_user = us_id
where ((us_auto_subscribe_own_bugs = 1 and bg_assigned_to_user = us_id)
or
(us_auto_subscribe_reported_bugs = 1 and bg_reported_user = us_id))
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and us_id not in

/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (4 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (4 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (4 <= us_assigned_notifications and 0 = bs_user)
or (4 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 214
and (us_id <> 3 or isnull(us_send_notifications_to_self,0) = 1)

/* get searchable cols */					
select sc.name
from syscolumns sc
inner join systypes st on st.xusertype = sc.xusertype
inner join sysobjects so on sc.id = so.id
where so.name = 'bugs'
and st.[name] <> 'sysname'
and sc.name not in ('rowguid',
'bg_id',
'bg_short_desc',
'bg_reported_user',
'bg_reported_date',
'bg_project',
'bg_org',
'bg_category',
'bg_priority',
'bg_status',
'bg_assigned_to_user',
'bg_last_updated_user',
'bg_last_updated_date',
'bg_user_defined_attribute',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3',
'bg_tags')
and st.[name] in ('nvarchar','varchar')
and sc.length > 30

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 214
and a.bp_parent is null
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
where us_active = 1
and og_can_be_assigned_to = 1
and (0 <> 0 or 4 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 0
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

 bg_short_desc [desc], isnull(pj_name,'') [project], isnull(og_name,'') [organization], isnull(ct_name,'') [category], rpt.us_username [reported by],
 bg_reported_date [reported on], isnull(pr_name,'') [priority], isnull(asg.us_username,'') [assigned to],
 isnull(st_name,'') [status], isnull(lu.us_username,'') [last updated by], bg_last_updated_date [last updated on]
 from bugs 
 left outer join bug_user on bu_bug = bg_id and bu_user = 3 
 left outer join users rpt on rpt.us_id = bg_reported_user
 left outer join users asg on asg.us_id = bg_assigned_to_user
 left outer join users lu on lu.us_id = bg_last_updated_user

 left outer join orgs on og_id = bg_org
 left outer join categories on ct_id = bg_category
 left outer join priorities on pr_id = bg_priority
 left outer join statuses on st_id = bg_status

					select pu_project
					from project_user_xref
					where pu_user = 3
					and pu_permission_level = 0)) 
					    and bugs.bg_org = 4  ) order by bg_id desc

select '#ffffff', bg_id [id], bg_short_desc [desc] ,
	temp_source [search_source] ,
	temp_text [search_text],
	bg_reported_date [date],
	isnull(st_name,'') [status],
	temp_score [$SCORE]
from bugs
inner join #f22d012d4c3e4dc1968ecb2b23d126ee t on t.temp_bg_id = bg_id and t.temp_bp_id = 0
left outer join statuses on st_id = bg_status
where /* ALTER_HERE */  (bugs.bg_project not in (
					select pu_project
					from project_user_xref
					where pu_user = 3
					and pu_permission_level = 0)) 
					    and bugs.bg_org = 4 

union

select '#ffffff', bg_id, bg_short_desc,
	bp_type + ',' + convert(varchar,bp_id) COLLATE DATABASE_DEFAULT,
	temp_text,
	bp_date,
	isnull(st_name,''),
	temp_score
from bugs
inner join #f22d012d4c3e4dc1968ecb2b23d126ee t on t.temp_bg_id = bg_id
inner join bug_posts on temp_bp_id = bp_id
left outer join statuses on st_id = bg_status
where /* ALTER_HERE */  (bugs.bg_project not in (
					select pu_project
					from project_user_xref
					where pu_user = 3
					and pu_permission_level = 0)) 
					    and bugs.bg_org = 4 

order by t.temp_score desc, bg_id desc

/* check session */
declare @project_admin int
select @project_admin = count(1)
	from sessions
	inner join project_user_xref on pu_user = se_user
	and pu_admin = 1
	where se_id = '4485040b-59c5-457f-8efa-b4309e3e69dd';

select us_id, us_admin,
us_username, us_firstname, us_lastname,
isnull(us_email,'') us_email,
isnull(us_bugs_per_page,10) us_bugs_per_page,
isnull(us_forced_project,0) us_forced_project,
us_use_fckeditor,
us_enable_bug_list_popups,
og.*,
isnull(us_forced_project, 0 ) us_forced_project,
isnull(pu_permission_level, 2) pu_permission_level,
@project_admin [project_admin]
from sessions
inner join users on se_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
left outer join project_user_xref
	on pu_project = us_forced_project
	and pu_user = us_id
where se_id = '4485040b-59c5-457f-8efa-b4309e3e69dd'
and us_active = 1

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 166
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 and a.bp_hidden_from_external_users = 0
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

 /* get_bug_datarow */
if not exists (select bu_bug from bug_user where bu_bug = 166 and bu_user = 3)
	insert into bug_user (bu_bug, bu_user, bu_flag, bu_seen, bu_vote) values(166, 3, 0, 1, 0)

declare @svn_revisions int
declare @git_commits int
declare @hg_revisions int
declare @tasks int
declare @related int;
set @svn_revisions = 0
set @git_commits = 0
set @hg_revisions = 0
set @tasks = 0
set @related = 0

select bg_id [id],
bg_short_desc [short_desc],
isnull(bg_tags,'') [bg_tags],
isnull(ru.us_username,'[deleted user]') [reporter],
isnull(ru.us_email,'') [reporter_email],
case rtrim(ru.us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(ru.us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(ru.us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(ru.us_lastname + ', ' + ru.us_firstname,'')
	end [reporter_fullname],
bg_reported_date [reported_date],
datediff(s,bg_reported_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
isnull(lu.us_username,'') [last_updated_user],
case rtrim(lu.us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(lu.us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(lu.us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(lu.us_lastname + ', ' + lu.us_firstname,'')
	end [last_updated_fullname],


bg_last_updated_date [last_updated_date],
isnull(bg_project,0) [project],
isnull(pj_name,'[no project]') [current_project],

isnull(bg_org,0) [organization],
isnull(bugorg.og_name,'') [og_name],

isnull(bg_category,0) [category],
isnull(ct_name,'') [category_name],

isnull(bg_priority,0) [priority],
isnull(pr_name,'') [priority_name],

isnull(bg_status,0) [status],
isnull(st_name,'') [status_name],

isnull(bg_user_defined_attribute,0) [udf],
isnull(udf_name,'') [udf_name],

isnull(bg_assigned_to_user,0) [assigned_to_user],
isnull(asg.us_username,'[not assigned]') [assigned_to_username],
case rtrim(asg.us_firstname)
when null then isnull(asg.us_lastname, '[not assigned]')
when '' then isnull(asg.us_lastname, '[not assigned]')
else isnull(asg.us_lastname + ', ' + asg.us_firstname,'[not assigned]')
end [assigned_to_fullname],

isnull(bs_user,0) [subscribed],

case
when
	4 <> bg_org
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
		then userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
	isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end [pu_permission_level],

isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1],
isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2],
isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3],
@related [relationship_cnt],
@svn_revisions [svn_revision_cnt],
@git_commits [git_commit_cnt],
@hg_revisions [hg_commit_cnt],
@tasks [task_cnt],
getdate() [snapshot_timestamp]

from bugs
inner join users this_user on us_id = 3
inner join orgs userorg on this_user.us_org = userorg.og_id
left outer join user_defined_attribute on bg_user_defined_attribute = udf_id
left outer join projects on bg_project = pj_id
left outer join orgs bugorg on bg_org = bugorg.og_id
left outer join categories on bg_category = ct_id
left outer join priorities on bg_priority = pr_id
left outer join statuses on bg_status = st_id
left outer join users asg on bg_assigned_to_user = asg.us_id
left outer join users ru on bg_reported_user = ru.us_id
left outer join users lu on bg_last_updated_user = lu.us_id
left outer join bug_subscriptions on bs_bug = bg_id and bs_user = 3
left outer join project_user_xref on pj_id = pu_project
and pu_user = 3
where bg_id = 166

/* drop downs */ select pj_id, pj_name
		from projects
		left outer join project_user_xref on pj_id = pu_project
		and pu_user = 3
		where pj_active = 1
		and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) not in (0, 1)
		order by pj_name;
select og_id, og_name from orgs where og_active = 1 order by og_name;
select ct_id, ct_name from categories order by ct_sort_seq, ct_name;
select pr_id, pr_name from priorities order by pr_sort_seq, pr_name;
select st_id, st_name from statuses order by st_sort_seq, st_name;
select udf_id, udf_name from user_defined_attribute order by udf_sort_seq, udf_name;

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
where us_active = 1
and og_can_be_assigned_to = 1
and (0 <> 0 or 4 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 0
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

	from sessions
	inner join project_user_xref on pu_user = se_user
	and pu_admin = 1
	where se_id = '4485040b-59c5-457f-8efa-b4309e3e69dd';

us_enable_bug_list_popups,
og.*,
isnull(us_forced_project, 0 ) us_forced_project,
isnull(pu_permission_level, 2) pu_permission_level,
@project_admin [project_admin]
from sessions

declare @pj int
select @pj = bg_project from bugs where bg_id = 166

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 166
and bs_user in
(select x.pu_user
from projects
left outer join project_user_xref x on pu_project = pj_id
where pu_project = @pj
and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) = 0)

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 166
and bs_user in
(select us_id from users
 inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
 inner join bugs on bg_id = 166
 where og_other_orgs_permission_level = 0
 and bg_org <> og_id)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 166, us_id
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = 166
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_project = @pj and pu_user = us_id
where us_auto_subscribe = 1
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and us_id not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 166)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 166, pj_default_user
from projects
inner join users on pj_default_user = us_id
where pj_id = @pj
and pj_default_user <> 0
and pj_auto_subscribe_default_user = 1
and us_active = 1
and pj_default_user not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 166)

	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and pu_project = @pj
and pu_user not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 166)

/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (2 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_assigned_notifications and 0 = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 166
and (us_id <> 3 or isnull(us_send_notifications_to_self,0) = 1)

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 166
and a.bp_parent is null
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

/* get searchable cols */					
select sc.name
from syscolumns sc
inner join systypes st on st.xusertype = sc.xusertype
inner join sysobjects so on sc.id = so.id
where so.name = 'bugs'
and st.[name] <> 'sysname'
and sc.name not in ('rowguid',
'bg_id',
'bg_short_desc',
'bg_reported_user',
'bg_reported_date',
'bg_project',
'bg_org',
'bg_category',
'bg_priority',
'bg_status',
'bg_assigned_to_user',
'bg_last_updated_user',
'bg_last_updated_date',
'bg_user_defined_attribute',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3',
'bg_tags')
and st.[name] in ('nvarchar','varchar')
and sc.length > 30

	insert into bug_user (bu_bug, bu_user, bu_flag, bu_seen, bu_vote) values(166, 3, 0, 1, 0) 
update bug_user set bu_seen = 1, bu_seen_datetime = getdate() where bu_bug = 166 and bu_user = 3 and bu_seen <> 1
declare @svn_revisions int
declare @git_commits int
declare @hg_revisions int
declare @tasks int
declare @related int;
set @svn_revisions = 0
set @git_commits = 0
set @hg_revisions = 0
set @tasks = 0
set @related = 0

select bg_id [id],
bg_short_desc [short_desc],
isnull(bg_tags,'') [bg_tags],
isnull(ru.us_username,'[deleted user]') [reporter],
isnull(ru.us_email,'') [reporter_email],
case rtrim(ru.us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(ru.us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(ru.us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(ru.us_lastname + ', ' + ru.us_firstname,'')
	end [reporter_fullname],
bg_reported_date [reported_date],
datediff(s,bg_reported_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
isnull(lu.us_username,'') [last_updated_user],
case rtrim(lu.us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(lu.us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(lu.us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(lu.us_lastname + ', ' + lu.us_firstname,'')
	end [last_updated_fullname],


bg_last_updated_date [last_updated_date],
isnull(bg_project,0) [project],
isnull(pj_name,'[no project]') [current_project],

isnull(bg_org,0) [organization],
isnull(bugorg.og_name,'') [og_name],

isnull(bg_category,0) [category],
isnull(ct_name,'') [category_name],

isnull(bg_priority,0) [priority],
isnull(pr_name,'') [priority_name],

isnull(bg_status,0) [status],
isnull(st_name,'') [status_name],

isnull(bg_user_defined_attribute,0) [udf],
isnull(udf_name,'') [udf_name],

isnull(bg_assigned_to_user,0) [assigned_to_user],
isnull(asg.us_username,'[not assigned]') [assigned_to_username],
case rtrim(asg.us_firstname)
when null then isnull(asg.us_lastname, '[not assigned]')
when '' then isnull(asg.us_lastname, '[not assigned]')
else isnull(asg.us_lastname + ', ' + asg.us_firstname,'[not assigned]')
end [assigned_to_fullname],

isnull(bs_user,0) [subscribed],

case
when
	4 <> bg_org
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
		then userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
	isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end [pu_permission_level],

isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1],
isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2],
isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3],
@related [relationship_cnt],
@svn_revisions [svn_revision_cnt],
@git_commits [git_commit_cnt],
@hg_revisions [hg_commit_cnt],
@tasks [task_cnt],
getdate() [snapshot_timestamp]

from bugs
inner join users this_user on us_id = 3
inner join orgs userorg on this_user.us_org = userorg.og_id
left outer join user_defined_attribute on bg_user_defined_attribute = udf_id
left outer join projects on bg_project = pj_id
left outer join orgs bugorg on bg_org = bugorg.og_id
left outer join categories on bg_category = ct_id
left outer join priorities on bg_priority = pr_id
left outer join statuses on bg_status = st_id
left outer join users asg on bg_assigned_to_user = asg.us_id
left outer join users ru on bg_reported_user = ru.us_id
left outer join users lu on bg_last_updated_user = lu.us_id
left outer join bug_subscriptions on bs_bug = bg_id and bs_user = 3
left outer join project_user_xref on pj_id = pu_project
and pu_user = 3
where bg_id = 166

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
where us_active = 1
and og_can_be_assigned_to = 1
and (0 <> 0 or 4 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 0
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 166
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 and a.bp_hidden_from_external_users = 0
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

/* check session */
declare @project_admin int
select @project_admin = count(1)
	from sessions
	inner join project_user_xref on pu_user = se_user
	and pu_admin = 1
	where se_id = '4485040b-59c5-457f-8efa-b4309e3e69dd';

select us_id, us_admin,
us_username, us_firstname, us_lastname,
isnull(us_email,'') us_email,
isnull(us_bugs_per_page,10) us_bugs_per_page,
isnull(us_forced_project,0) us_forced_project,
us_use_fckeditor,
us_enable_bug_list_popups,
og.*,
isnull(us_forced_project, 0 ) us_forced_project,
isnull(pu_permission_level, 2) pu_permission_level,
@project_admin [project_admin]
from sessions
inner join users on se_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
left outer join project_user_xref
	on pu_project = us_forced_project
	and pu_user = us_id
where se_id = '4485040b-59c5-457f-8efa-b4309e3e69dd'
and us_active = 1

 bg_short_desc [desc], isnull(pj_name,'') [project], isnull(og_name,'') [organization], isnull(ct_name,'') [category], rpt.us_username [reported by],
 bg_reported_date [reported on], isnull(pr_name,'') [priority], isnull(asg.us_username,'') [assigned to],
 isnull(st_name,'') [status], isnull(lu.us_username,'') [last updated by], bg_last_updated_date [last updated on]
 from bugs 
 left outer join bug_user on bu_bug = bg_id and bu_user = 3 
 left outer join users rpt on rpt.us_id = bg_reported_user
 left outer join users asg on asg.us_id = bg_assigned_to_user
 left outer join users lu on lu.us_id = bg_last_updated_user
 left outer join projects on pj_id = bg_project
 left outer join orgs on og_id = bg_org
 left outer join categories on ct_id = bg_category
 left outer join priorities on pr_id = bg_priority
 left outer join statuses on st_id = bg_status

					select pu_project
					from project_user_xref
					where pu_user = 3
					and pu_permission_level = 0)) 
					    and bugs.bg_org = 4  ) order by bg_id desc

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 213
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 and a.bp_hidden_from_external_users = 0
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

/* check session */
declare @project_admin int
select @project_admin = count(1)
	from sessions
	inner join project_user_xref on pu_user = se_user
	and pu_admin = 1
	where se_id = '4485040b-59c5-457f-8efa-b4309e3e69dd';

select us_id, us_admin,
us_username, us_firstname, us_lastname,
isnull(us_email,'') us_email,
isnull(us_bugs_per_page,10) us_bugs_per_page,
isnull(us_forced_project,0) us_forced_project,
us_use_fckeditor,
us_enable_bug_list_popups,
og.*,
isnull(us_forced_project, 0 ) us_forced_project,
isnull(pu_permission_level, 2) pu_permission_level,
@project_admin [project_admin]
from sessions
inner join users on se_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
left outer join project_user_xref
	on pu_project = us_forced_project
	and pu_user = us_id
where se_id = '4485040b-59c5-457f-8efa-b4309e3e69dd'
and us_active = 1

 /* get_bug_datarow */
if not exists (select bu_bug from bug_user where bu_bug = 0 and bu_user = 3)
	insert into bug_user (bu_bug, bu_user, bu_flag, bu_seen, bu_vote) values(0, 3, 0, 1, 0) 
update bug_user set bu_seen = 1, bu_seen_datetime = getdate() where bu_bug = 0 and bu_user = 3 and bu_seen <> 1
declare @svn_revisions int
declare @git_commits int
declare @hg_revisions int
declare @tasks int
declare @related int;
set @svn_revisions = 0
set @git_commits = 0
set @hg_revisions = 0
set @tasks = 0
set @related = 0

select bg_id [id],
bg_short_desc [short_desc],
isnull(bg_tags,'') [bg_tags],
isnull(ru.us_username,'[deleted user]') [reporter],
isnull(ru.us_email,'') [reporter_email],
case rtrim(ru.us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(ru.us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(ru.us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(ru.us_lastname + ', ' + ru.us_firstname,'')
	end [reporter_fullname],
bg_reported_date [reported_date],
datediff(s,bg_reported_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
isnull(lu.us_username,'') [last_updated_user],
case rtrim(lu.us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(lu.us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(lu.us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(lu.us_lastname + ', ' + lu.us_firstname,'')
	end [last_updated_fullname],


bg_last_updated_date [last_updated_date],
isnull(bg_project,0) [project],
isnull(pj_name,'[no project]') [current_project],

isnull(bg_org,0) [organization],
isnull(bugorg.og_name,'') [og_name],

isnull(bg_category,0) [category],
isnull(ct_name,'') [category_name],

isnull(bg_priority,0) [priority],
isnull(pr_name,'') [priority_name],

isnull(bg_status,0) [status],
isnull(st_name,'') [status_name],

isnull(bg_user_defined_attribute,0) [udf],
isnull(udf_name,'') [udf_name],

isnull(bg_assigned_to_user,0) [assigned_to_user],
isnull(asg.us_username,'[not assigned]') [assigned_to_username],
case rtrim(asg.us_firstname)
when null then isnull(asg.us_lastname, '[not assigned]')
when '' then isnull(asg.us_lastname, '[not assigned]')
else isnull(asg.us_lastname + ', ' + asg.us_firstname,'[not assigned]')
end [assigned_to_fullname],

isnull(bs_user,0) [subscribed],

case
when
	4 <> bg_org
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
		then userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
	isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end [pu_permission_level],

isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1],
isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2],
isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3],
@related [relationship_cnt],
@svn_revisions [svn_revision_cnt],
@git_commits [git_commit_cnt],
@hg_revisions [hg_commit_cnt],
@tasks [task_cnt],
getdate() [snapshot_timestamp]

from bugs
inner join users this_user on us_id = 3
inner join orgs userorg on this_user.us_org = userorg.og_id
left outer join user_defined_attribute on bg_user_defined_attribute = udf_id
left outer join projects on bg_project = pj_id
left outer join orgs bugorg on bg_org = bugorg.og_id
left outer join categories on bg_category = ct_id
left outer join priorities on bg_priority = pr_id
left outer join statuses on bg_status = st_id
left outer join users asg on bg_assigned_to_user = asg.us_id
left outer join users ru on bg_reported_user = ru.us_id
left outer join users lu on bg_last_updated_user = lu.us_id
left outer join bug_subscriptions on bs_bug = bg_id and bs_user = 3
left outer join project_user_xref on pj_id = pu_project
and pu_user = 3
where bg_id = 0

declare @pj int
select @pj = bg_project from bugs where bg_id = 215

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 215
and bs_user in
(select x.pu_user
from projects
left outer join project_user_xref x on pu_project = pj_id
where pu_project = @pj
and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) = 0)

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 215
and bs_user in
(select us_id from users
 inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
 inner join bugs on bg_id = 215
 where og_other_orgs_permission_level = 0
 and bg_org <> og_id)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 215, us_id
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = 215
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_project = @pj and pu_user = us_id
where us_auto_subscribe = 1
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and us_id not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 215)

(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions

/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (1 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (1 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (1 <= us_assigned_notifications and 0 = bs_user)
or (1 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 215
and (us_id <> 3 or isnull(us_send_notifications_to_self,0) = 1)

a.bp_comment,

	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')

	end [us_fullname],

a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 215
and a.bp_parent is null
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

select isnull(pr_background_color,'#ffffff'), bg_id [id], isnull(bu_flag,0) [$FLAG], 
 bg_short_desc [desc], isnull(pj_name,'') [project], isnull(og_name,'') [organization], isnull(ct_name,'') [category], rpt.us_username [reported by],
 bg_reported_date [reported on], isnull(pr_name,'') [priority], isnull(asg.us_username,'') [assigned to],
 isnull(st_name,'') [status], isnull(lu.us_username,'') [last updated by], bg_last_updated_date [last updated on]
 from bugs 
 left outer join bug_user on bu_bug = bg_id and bu_user = 3 
 left outer join users rpt on rpt.us_id = bg_reported_user
 left outer join users asg on asg.us_id = bg_assigned_to_user
 left outer join users lu on lu.us_id = bg_last_updated_user
 left outer join projects on pj_id = bg_project

a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],

a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 214
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 and a.bp_hidden_from_external_users = 0
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username

and (0 <> 0 or 4 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 0
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

declare @pj int
select @pj = bg_project from bugs where bg_id = 214

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 214
and bs_user in
(select x.pu_user
from projects
left outer join project_user_xref x on pu_project = pj_id
where pu_project = @pj
and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) = 0)

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 214
and bs_user in
(select us_id from users
 inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
 inner join bugs on bg_id = 214
 where og_other_orgs_permission_level = 0
 and bg_org <> og_id)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 214, us_id
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = 214
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_project = @pj and pu_user = us_id
where us_auto_subscribe = 1
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and us_id not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 214)

from projects

where pj_id = @pj
and pj_default_user <> 0
and pj_auto_subscribe_default_user = 1
and us_active = 1
and pj_default_user not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 214)
