/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (4 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (4 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (4 <= us_assigned_notifications and 0 = bs_user)
or (4 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 214
and (us_id <> 3 or isnull(us_send_notifications_to_self,0) = 1)

/* get searchable cols */					
select sc.name
from syscolumns sc
inner join systypes st on st.xusertype = sc.xusertype
inner join sysobjects so on sc.id = so.id
where so.name = 'bugs'
and st.[name] <> 'sysname'
and sc.name not in ('rowguid',
'bg_id',
'bg_short_desc',
'bg_reported_user',
'bg_reported_date',
'bg_project',
'bg_org',
'bg_category',
'bg_priority',
'bg_status',
'bg_assigned_to_user',
'bg_last_updated_user',
'bg_last_updated_date',
'bg_user_defined_attribute',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3',
'bg_tags')
and st.[name] in ('nvarchar','varchar')
and sc.length > 30

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 214
and a.bp_parent is null
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
where us_active = 1
and og_can_be_assigned_to = 1
and (0 <> 0 or 4 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 0
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

declare @project_admin int
select @project_admin = count(1)
	from sessions
	inner join project_user_xref on pu_user = se_user
	and pu_admin = 1
	where se_id = '4485040b-59c5-457f-8efa-b4309e3e69dd';

select us_id, us_admin,
us_username, us_firstname, us_lastname,
isnull(us_email,'') us_email,

isnull(us_forced_project,0) us_forced_project,
us_use_fckeditor,
us_enable_bug_list_popups,
og.*,
isnull(us_forced_project, 0 ) us_forced_project,
isnull(pu_permission_level, 2) pu_permission_level,
@project_admin [project_admin]
from sessions
inner join users on se_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
left outer join project_user_xref
	on pu_project = us_forced_project
	and pu_user = us_id

declare @now datetime
		declare @last_updated datetime
		select @last_updated = bg_last_updated_date from bugs where bg_id = 214
		if @last_updated > '20160415 18:15:14:967'
		begin
			-- signal that we did NOT do the update
			set @now = '20160415 18:15:14:967'
		end
		else

			-- signal that we DID do the update

declare @pj int
select @pj = bg_project from bugs where bg_id = 214

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 214
and bs_user in
(select x.pu_user
from projects
left outer join project_user_xref x on pu_project = pj_id
where pu_project = @pj
and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) = 0)

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 214
and bs_user in
(select us_id from users
 inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
 inner join bugs on bg_id = 214
 where og_other_orgs_permission_level = 0
 and bg_org <> og_id)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 214, us_id
from users

/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (4 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (4 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (4 <= us_assigned_notifications and 0 = bs_user)
or (4 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 214
and (us_id <> 3 or isnull(us_send_notifications_to_self,0) = 1)

select @pj = bg_project from bugs where bg_id = 214

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 214
and bs_user in
(select x.pu_user
from projects
left outer join project_user_xref x on pu_project = pj_id
where pu_project = @pj
and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) = 0)

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 214
and bs_user in
(select us_id from users
 inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
 inner join bugs on bg_id = 214
 where og_other_orgs_permission_level = 0
 and bg_org <> og_id)

select 214, us_id
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = 214
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_project = @pj and pu_user = us_id
where us_auto_subscribe = 1

	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and us_id not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 214)

/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (4 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (4 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (4 <= us_assigned_notifications and 0 = bs_user)
or (4 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 214

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
where us_active = 1
and og_can_be_assigned_to = 1
and (0 <> 0 or 4 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 0
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

 bg_short_desc [desc], isnull(pj_name,'') [project], isnull(og_name,'') [organization], isnull(ct_name,'') [category], rpt.us_username [reported by],
 bg_reported_date [reported on], isnull(pr_name,'') [priority], isnull(asg.us_username,'') [assigned to],
 isnull(st_name,'') [status], isnull(lu.us_username,'') [last updated by], bg_last_updated_date [last updated on]
 from bugs

 left outer join users asg on asg.us_id = bg_assigned_to_user

 left outer join orgs on og_id = bg_org
 left outer join categories on ct_id = bg_category
 left outer join priorities on pr_id = bg_priority

					select pu_project

					where pu_user = 3
					and pu_permission_level = 0))

/* check session */
declare @project_admin int
select @project_admin = count(1)
	from sessions
	inner join project_user_xref on pu_user = se_user
	and pu_admin = 1
	where se_id = '4485040b-59c5-457f-8efa-b4309e3e69dd';

select us_id, us_admin,
us_username, us_firstname, us_lastname,
isnull(us_email,'') us_email,
isnull(us_bugs_per_page,10) us_bugs_per_page,
isnull(us_forced_project,0) us_forced_project,
us_use_fckeditor,
us_enable_bug_list_popups,
og.*,
isnull(us_forced_project, 0 ) us_forced_project,
isnull(pu_permission_level, 2) pu_permission_level,
@project_admin [project_admin]
from sessions
inner join users on se_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
left outer join project_user_xref
	on pu_project = us_forced_project
	and pu_user = us_id
where se_id = '4485040b-59c5-457f-8efa-b4309e3e69dd'
and us_active = 1
2016-04-15 18:17:58 http://www.learncodinganywhere.com/bugtracker/ajax.aspx?bugid=208 elapsed milliseconds:0001

bg_org

on pu_project = bg_project

2016-04-15 18:17:58 http://www.learncodinganywhere.com/bugtracker/ajax.aspx?bugid=208 elapsed milliseconds:0000
2016-04-15 18:17:58 http://www.learncodinganywhere.com/bugtracker/ajax.aspx?bugid=208 sql=

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 208
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 and a.bp_hidden_from_external_users = 0
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id
2016-04-15 18:17:58 http://www.learncodinganywhere.com/bugtracker/ajax.aspx?bugid=208 elapsed milliseconds:0000

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 208
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 and a.bp_hidden_from_external_users = 0
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

		from projects
		left outer join project_user_xref on pj_id = pu_project

select st_id, st_name from statuses order by st_sort_seq, st_name;

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
where us_active = 1
and og_can_be_assigned_to = 1
and (0 <> 0 or 4 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 0
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

declare @now datetime
		declare @last_updated datetime
		select @last_updated = bg_last_updated_date from bugs where bg_id = 215
		if @last_updated > '20160415 18:26:59:413'

declare @pj int
select @pj = bg_project from bugs where bg_id = 215

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 215
and bs_user in
(select x.pu_user
from projects
left outer join project_user_xref x on pu_project = pj_id
where pu_project = @pj
and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) = 0)

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 215
and bs_user in
(select us_id from users
 inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
 inner join bugs on bg_id = 215
 where og_other_orgs_permission_level = 0
 and bg_org <> og_id)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 215, us_id
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = 215
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_project = @pj and pu_user = us_id
where us_auto_subscribe = 1
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and us_id not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 215)

from projects
inner join users on pj_default_user = us_id
where pj_id = @pj
and pj_default_user <> 0
and pj_auto_subscribe_default_user = 1
and us_active = 1
and pj_default_user not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 215)

/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (2 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_assigned_notifications and 0 = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 215
and (us_id <> 3 or isnull(us_send_notifications_to_self,0) = 1)

inner join systypes st on st.xusertype = sc.xusertype

	4 <> bg_org

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 215
and a.bp_parent is null
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug

and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 and a.bp_hidden_from_external_users = 0
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

 bg_short_desc [desc], isnull(pj_name,'') [project], isnull(og_name,'') [organization], isnull(ct_name,'') [category], rpt.us_username [reported by],
 bg_reported_date [reported on], isnull(pr_name,'') [priority], isnull(asg.us_username,'') [assigned to],
 isnull(st_name,'') [status], isnull(lu.us_username,'') [last updated by], bg_last_updated_date [last updated on]
 from bugs 
 left outer join bug_user on bu_bug = bg_id and bu_user = 3 
 left outer join users rpt on rpt.us_id = bg_reported_user
 left outer join users asg on asg.us_id = bg_assigned_to_user

 left outer join orgs on og_id = bg_org

 left outer join priorities on pr_id = bg_priority

					where pu_user = 3

/* check session */
declare @project_admin int
select @project_admin = count(1)
	from sessions
	inner join project_user_xref on pu_user = se_user
	and pu_admin = 1
	where se_id = '4485040b-59c5-457f-8efa-b4309e3e69dd';

select us_id, us_admin,
us_username, us_firstname, us_lastname,
isnull(us_email,'') us_email,
isnull(us_bugs_per_page,10) us_bugs_per_page,
isnull(us_forced_project,0) us_forced_project,
us_use_fckeditor,
us_enable_bug_list_popups,
og.*,
isnull(us_forced_project, 0 ) us_forced_project,
isnull(pu_permission_level, 2) pu_permission_level,
@project_admin [project_admin]
from sessions
inner join users on se_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
left outer join project_user_xref
	on pu_project = us_forced_project
	and pu_user = us_id
where se_id = '4485040b-59c5-457f-8efa-b4309e3e69dd'
and us_active = 1

select isnull(pr_background_color,'#ffffff'), bg_id [id], isnull(bu_flag,0) [$FLAG], 
 bg_short_desc [desc], isnull(pj_name,'') [project], isnull(og_name,'') [organization], isnull(ct_name,'') [category], rpt.us_username [reported by],
 bg_reported_date [reported on], isnull(pr_name,'') [priority], isnull(asg.us_username,'') [assigned to],
 isnull(st_name,'') [status], isnull(lu.us_username,'') [last updated by], bg_last_updated_date [last updated on]
 from bugs 
 left outer join bug_user on bu_bug = bg_id and bu_user = 3 
 left outer join users rpt on rpt.us_id = bg_reported_user
 left outer join users asg on asg.us_id = bg_assigned_to_user
 left outer join users lu on lu.us_id = bg_last_updated_user
 left outer join projects on pj_id = bg_project
 left outer join orgs on og_id = bg_org
 left outer join categories on ct_id = bg_category
 left outer join priorities on pr_id = bg_priority
 left outer join statuses on st_id = bg_status
 where /* altered - both  */ (  bg_status <> 5  ) AND (  (bugs.bg_project not in (
					select pu_project
					from project_user_xref
					where pu_user = 3
					and pu_permission_level = 0)) 
					    and bugs.bg_org = 4  ) order by bg_id desc

2016-04-15 18:46:09 http://www.learncodinganywhere.com/bugtracker/ajax.aspx?bugid=215 elapsed milliseconds:0000

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 215
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 and a.bp_hidden_from_external_users = 0
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id
2016-04-15 18:46:09 http://www.learncodinganywhere.com/bugtracker/ajax.aspx?bugid=215 elapsed milliseconds:0000

a.bp_type,

select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,

isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 215
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 and a.bp_hidden_from_external_users = 0
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

	when '' then isnull(ru.us_lastname, '')

	else isnull(lu.us_lastname + ', ' + lu.us_firstname,'')
	end [last_updated_fullname],

declare @pj int
select @pj = bg_project from bugs where bg_id = 216

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 216
and bs_user in
(select x.pu_user
from projects
left outer join project_user_xref x on pu_project = pj_id
where pu_project = @pj
and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) = 0)

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 216
and bs_user in
(select us_id from users
 inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
 inner join bugs on bg_id = 216
 where og_other_orgs_permission_level = 0
 and bg_org <> og_id)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 216, us_id
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = 216
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_project = @pj and pu_user = us_id
where us_auto_subscribe = 1
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and us_id not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 216)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 216, pj_default_user
from projects
inner join users on pj_default_user = us_id
where pj_id = @pj
and pj_default_user <> 0
and pj_auto_subscribe_default_user = 1
and us_active = 1
and pj_default_user not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 216)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 216, pu_user from project_user_xref
inner join users on pu_user = us_id
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = 216
where pu_auto_subscribe = 1
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and pu_project = @pj
and pu_user not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 216, us_id
from users
inner join bugs on bg_id = 216
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_project = @pj and pu_user = us_id

or
(us_auto_subscribe_reported_bugs = 1 and bg_reported_user = us_id))
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and us_id not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 216)

/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (1 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (1 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (1 <= us_assigned_notifications and 0 = bs_user)
or (1 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 216
and (us_id <> 3 or isnull(us_send_notifications_to_self,0) = 1)

isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,

isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a

left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug

 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

select st_id, st_name from statuses order by st_sort_seq, st_name;
select udf_id, udf_name from user_defined_attribute order by udf_sort_seq, udf_name;

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
where us_active = 1
and og_can_be_assigned_to = 1
and (0 <> 0 or 4 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 0
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

declare @now datetime
		declare @last_updated datetime
		select @last_updated = bg_last_updated_date from bugs where bg_id = 216
		if @last_updated > '20160415 19:25:04:200'
		begin
			-- signal that we did NOT do the update
			set @now = '20160415 19:25:04:200'
		end
		else
		begin
			-- signal that we DID do the update
			set @now = getdate()

			update bugs set

			bg_tags = N'',

declare @pj int
select @pj = bg_project from bugs where bg_id = 216

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 216
and bs_user in
(select x.pu_user
from projects
left outer join project_user_xref x on pu_project = pj_id
where pu_project = @pj
and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) = 0)

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 216
and bs_user in
(select us_id from users
 inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
 inner join bugs on bg_id = 216
 where og_other_orgs_permission_level = 0
 and bg_org <> og_id)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 216, us_id
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = 216
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_project = @pj and pu_user = us_id
where us_auto_subscribe = 1
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and us_id not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 216)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 216, pj_default_user
from projects
inner join users on pj_default_user = us_id
where pj_id = @pj
and pj_default_user <> 0
and pj_auto_subscribe_default_user = 1
and us_active = 1
and pj_default_user not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 216)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 216, pu_user from project_user_xref
inner join users on pu_user = us_id
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = 216
where pu_auto_subscribe = 1
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and pu_project = @pj
and pu_user not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 216)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 216, us_id
from users
inner join bugs on bg_id = 216
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_project = @pj and pu_user = us_id
where ((us_auto_subscribe_own_bugs = 1 and bg_assigned_to_user = us_id)
or
(us_auto_subscribe_reported_bugs = 1 and bg_reported_user = us_id))
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2

/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (4 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (4 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (4 <= us_assigned_notifications and 0 = bs_user)
or (4 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 216
and (us_id <> 3 or isnull(us_send_notifications_to_self,0) = 1)

select isnull(pr_background_color,'#ffffff'), bg_id [id], isnull(bu_flag,0) [$FLAG], 
 bg_short_desc [desc], isnull(pj_name,'') [project], isnull(og_name,'') [organization], isnull(ct_name,'') [category], rpt.us_username [reported by],
 bg_reported_date [reported on], isnull(pr_name,'') [priority], isnull(asg.us_username,'') [assigned to],
 isnull(st_name,'') [status], isnull(lu.us_username,'') [last updated by], bg_last_updated_date [last updated on]
 from bugs 
 left outer join bug_user on bu_bug = bg_id and bu_user = 3 
 left outer join users rpt on rpt.us_id = bg_reported_user
 left outer join users asg on asg.us_id = bg_assigned_to_user
 left outer join users lu on lu.us_id = bg_last_updated_user
 left outer join projects on pj_id = bg_project
 left outer join orgs on og_id = bg_org
 left outer join categories on ct_id = bg_category
 left outer join priorities on pr_id = bg_priority
 left outer join statuses on st_id = bg_status
 where /* altered - both  */ (  bg_status <> 5  ) AND (  (bugs.bg_project not in (
					select pu_project
					from project_user_xref
					where pu_user = 3
					and pu_permission_level = 0)) 
					    and bugs.bg_org = 4  ) order by bg_id desc

	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],

a.bp_date,

isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 216
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 and a.bp_hidden_from_external_users = 0
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) = 0)

/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (1 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (1 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (1 <= us_assigned_notifications and 0 = bs_user)
or (1 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 217
and (us_id <> 3 or isnull(us_send_notifications_to_self,0) = 1)

/* get searchable cols */					
select sc.name
from syscolumns sc
inner join systypes st on st.xusertype = sc.xusertype
inner join sysobjects so on sc.id = so.id

select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')

	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 217
and a.bp_parent is null
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
where us_active = 1
and og_can_be_assigned_to = 1
and (0 <> 0 or 4 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 0
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

2016-04-15 23:13:20  sql=

/* get searchable cols */					
select sc.name
from syscolumns sc
inner join systypes st on st.xusertype = sc.xusertype
inner join sysobjects so on sc.id = so.id
where so.name = 'bugs'
and st.[name] <> 'sysname'
and sc.name not in ('rowguid',
'bg_id',
'bg_short_desc',
'bg_reported_user',
'bg_reported_date',
'bg_project',
'bg_org',
'bg_category',
'bg_priority',
'bg_status',
'bg_assigned_to_user',
'bg_last_updated_user',
'bg_last_updated_date',
'bg_user_defined_attribute',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3',
'bg_tags')
and st.[name] in ('nvarchar','varchar')
and sc.length > 30

2016-04-15 23:13:20  sql=

create view votes_view as
select bu_bug as vote_bug, sum(bu_vote) as vote_total
from bug_user
group by bu_bug
having sum(bu_vote) > 0
